| TC-023 (state_edge) | WF-007 | Rapidly toggle Accounting Method to reveal/hide GL fields | User is on Share Products page, + Create Share Product wizard is opened, Reached Step 7 (Accounting) | 1. Observe the GL dropdown fields area for duplication, retained values, and any visible errors | When toggling to Cash-based the GL dropdown fields become visible; rapid toggling back to None hides them; toggling back to Cash-based re-displays the GL fields without creating duplicate UI elements or causing JS/render errors. Either previously entered GL values are preserved or cleared explicitly, but the UI remains consistent and no duplicate fields or console-level error messages are visible to the user. | medium |
| TC-024 (input_edge) |  | High-precision Nominal/Unit Price input vs Decimal Places setting | User is on Share Products page, + Create Share Product wizard is opened | 1. Observe the UI until the report results render or an error appears | Second submission attempt is blocked/ignored; only one Report_Results_Table render occurs for the request; the Run Report control shows a transient loading state and does not cause duplicate result tables or duplicate export jobs. | medium |
| TC-080 (data_edge) | WF-003 | Export to Excel when results table contains zero data rows (far-future date range) | User is logged in and on the Reports page, All tab is visible, A report has been run and Report_Results_Table is displayed with zero data rows | 1. | TC-081 (input_edge) | WF-001 | Run report with all parameter fields left blank (no filters) | User is logged in and on the Reports page, All tab is visible | 1. ## Account Transfers & Standing Instructions

Total: **24** (positive: 5, negative: 10, edge: 9)

### Positive Tests

| TC ID | WF Ref | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|--------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-001 | WF-001 | Process Account Transfer with sufficient balance | User logged in as <role>, Source account <From_Account> has available balance >= <transfer amount> | 1. Navigate to the Account Transfers page<br>2. Select <From_Office> in From Office<br>3. Select <From_Client> in From Client<br>4. Select <From_Account_Type> in From Account Type<br>5. Select <From_Account> in From Account<br>6. Select <To_Office> in To Office<br>7. Select <To_Client> in To Client<br>8. Select <To_Account_Type> in To Account Type<br>9. Select <To_Account> in To Account<br>10. Enter <transfer amount> in Transfer Amount (<= available balance)<br>11. Enter <transfer date> in Transfer Date<br>12. Enter <description> in Description (optional)<br>13. Click Submit | A success notification is shown with text: processes transfer; debits source account and credits destination account | high |
| TC-002 | WF-002 | Create a new Standing Instruction via top action | User logged in as <role> | 1. Navigate to the Standing Instructions page<br>2. Click + Create Standing Instruction<br>3. In the Create Standing Instruction form, enter <Name> in Name (required)<br>4. Select <From_Account> in From Account (optional)<br>5. Select <To_Account> in To Account (optional)<br>6. Select <Instruction_Type> in Instruction Type<br>7. If Instruction Type is Fixed, enter <Amount> in Amount (optional)<br>8. Enter <validity from date> in Validity From (optional) and <validity till date> in Validity Till (optional)<br>9. Select <Recurrence_Type> in Recurrence Type (optional) and fill Recurrence Frequency/Interval as <values> if Periodic<br>10. Click Create | A success notification is shown with text: creates standing instruction; a new row appears in the Standing Instructions table with Name = <Name> | high |
| TC-003 | WF-003 | Enable a Disabled Standing Instruction from the listing | User logged in as <role>, A standing instruction exists with Name = <Name> and Status = Disabled | 1. | TC-020 (state_edge) | WF-003 | Attempt to Enable a Standing Instruction that is already Active — is blocked / error shown | There is a standing instruction listed with Status = Active | 1. | TC-021 (state_edge) | WF-004 | Attempt to Disable a Standing Instruction that is already Disabled — is blocked / error shown | There is a standing instruction listed with Status = Disabled | 1. Click the row action 'Disable' | Disable action is blocked; the UI either disables/hides the Disable control for that row or displays an inline message indicating the instruction cannot be disabled because it is already Disabled (is blocked / error shown) | medium |
| TC-022 (interaction_edge) |  | Rapid consecutive state transitions on a standing instruction (Enable then immediate Disable) — second transition blocked to prevent race | There is a standing instruction listed with Status = Disabled, User can see row actions for Enable and Disable | 1. Open Standing Instructions table<br>2. Locate the row with Status = Disabled<br>3. Click 'Enable' on that row<br>4. Immediately (without waiting for UI refresh) click 'Disable' on the same row | The first action (Enable) succeeds and changes status to Active; the immediate second action (Disable) is blocked or results in a single consistent outcome with a visible message preventing conflicting transitions (is blocked / error shown) so the UI does not produce an inconsistent state | medium |
| TC-023 (input_edge) | WF-002 | Create Standing Instruction with Name longer than typical limits (>200 characters) — acceptance vs explicit error | User is on Create Standing Instruction form | 1. Click '+ Create Standing Instruction' to open the form<br>2. Enter a Name string of <more than 200 characters> into Name<br>3. Fill other required fields (if any) minimally to allow creation<br>4. Click Create | Either: the form accepts the long Name and the standing instruction is created with the Name displayed exactly as entered (succeeds); OR the Name field shows a visible inline error indicating the Name exceeds the maximum allowed length and creation is blocked (is blocked / error shown). The UI must provide a clear visible outcome (created record or inline error). | low |
| TC-024 (input_edge) | WF-002 | Create Standing Instruction with leading/trailing whitespace in Name — whitespace trimming behavior | User is on Create Standing Instruction form | 1. Click '+ Create Standing Instruction' to open the form<br>2. Enter Name with leading and trailing spaces (e.g., '   <Name>   ')<br>3. Fill other required fields minimally<br>4. Click Create<br>5. Return to Standing Instructions table/listing | If the system trims whitespace: standing instruction creation succeeds and the Name shown in the listing is trimmed (no leading/trailing spaces) (succeeds). The listing must clearly show the final stored Name if created. | low |

| TC-039 (boundary) | WF-013 | Move_Down boundary: attempt to move down the last code value in the Code Values editor | User has opened Manage Codes and opened a Code Values Editor for a code list with at least one value, The code values list has a clearly identifiable last/bottom entry | 1. In the Code Values Editor, locate the last/bottom entry in the list<br>2. Click the Move_Down action for that last/bottom entry | The Move_Down action is blocked for the last/bottom entry; the UI shows no change in ordering and displays a visible message or disables the action for that entry (is blocked / error shown) | medium |
| TC-040 (input_edge) | WF-009 | Add_Value with very long Entry_Value (200+ characters) in Code Values editor | User has opened Manage Codes and opened a Code Values Editor for a code list, Add_Value action is available | 1. | TC-041 (interaction_edge) | WF-017 | Create Data Table: add several Column_Definitions then remove all and submit (repeating_group min=0 boundary) | User is on Create_Data_Table_Form, Column_Definitions repeating group initial state has zero items | 1. Repeat step 1 and 2 for multiple items (add more than one entry)<br>4. Remove each Column_Definitions item until zero items remain<br>5. | TC-042 (state_edge) | WF-019 | Attempt Approve when maker-checker configuration is disabled (precondition boundary) | User is on Global Configuration page, maker-checker configuration is set to Disabled (Enabled toggle is off), User navigates to Audit Trails page and locates an entry with Processing Result == Pending | 1. | TC-043 (data_edge) |  | Audit Trails filters: set Date_From equal to Date_To (same-day range) — boundary pass | User is on Audit Trails page with filters visible, There exist audit trail entries on the selected date | 1. | TC-044 (data_edge) |  | Audit Trails filters: set Date_From one day after Date_To (out-of-order) — boundary fail | User is on Audit Trails page with filters visible | 1. ## Logout

Total: **11** (positive: 3, negative: 4, edge: 4)

### Positive Tests

| TC ID | WF Ref | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|--------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-001 | WF-001 | Open Profile Settings via Profile Icon | User logged in as <role> | 1. Click the Profile Icon in the top-right corner to open the User Profile Menu<br>2. Click 'Profile Settings' in the dropdown | navigates to Profile Settings page | medium |
| TC-002 | WF-002 | Log Out via Profile Icon | User logged in as <role> | 1. Click the Profile Icon in the top-right corner to open the User Profile Menu<br>2. Click 'Log Out' in the dropdown | terminates authenticated session; clears authentication token; redirects to login page | high |
| TC-003 |  | Unauthenticated navigation to a protected page redirects to login | User not authenticated (logged out) | 1. Enter <authenticated page URL> in the browser address bar and navigate to it | redirects to login page | medium |

### Negative Tests

| TC ID | WF Ref | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|--------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-004 |  | Profile icon/menu inaccessible when unauthenticated | User is not logged in | 1. Open the application home page while not logged in<br>2. Click the top-right Profile Icon | Profile Icon and profile menu are not available: the Profile Icon is not visible in the top-right; no dropdown opens; 'Profile Settings' and 'Log Out' options are not present or accessible. The user remains on the public/unauthenticated page (no authenticated UI is shown). | high |
| TC-005 | WF-001 | Direct navigation to Profile Settings while unauthenticated is blocked | User is not logged in | 1. In the browser address bar, navigate to the Profile Settings page URL | Auth Guard blocks access: browser is redirected to the Login page; Profile Settings content is not displayed and no profile settings UI elements are visible. | high |
| TC-006 | WF-002 | Invoking Log Out endpoint while unauthenticated is blocked | User is not logged in | 1. In the browser address bar, navigate to the Log Out endpoint/URL that the 'Log Out' button would call | Precondition prevents logout action: browser is redirected to the Login page; no logout success behavior occurs (no authenticated session existed and no session changes happen). | high |
| TC-007 |  | Using browser Back after Log Out does not return to authenticated pages | User has an active authenticated session | 1. Open the Login page<br>2. Enter <valid credentials> in the Username/Email field<br>3. Enter <valid password> in the Password field<br>4. Click the Login button<br>5. Navigate to a protected page (e.g., Dashboard) while logged in<br>6. Click the Profile Icon<br>7. Click the 'Log Out' button in the profile menu<br>8. After the application redirects to the Login page, click the browser Back button to return to the previously viewed protected page | After logout the protected page remains inaccessible: Auth Guard immediately redirects to the Login page; protected page content is not displayed; the user remains logged out (authentication token/session cleared). | high |

### Edge & Boundary Tests

| TC ID | WF Ref | Test Case | Preconditions | Steps | Expected Result | Priority |
|-------|--------|-----------|---------------|-------|-----------------|----------|
| TC-008 (interaction_edge) | WF-002 | Rapid double-click Log Out | User is logged in | 1. Log in as a valid user<br>2. Click the Profile Icon in the top-right corner<br>3. Click the "Log Out" button<br>4. Immediately click the "Log Out" button again | First click succeeds: authenticated session is terminated and the user is redirected to the login page. The immediate second click is ignored (no additional navigation or error shown) and only a single logout action takes effect. | medium |
| TC-009 (interaction_edge) | WF-002 | Browser Back after Log Out should not return to protected page | User is logged in, User is on a protected page (e.g., dashboard) | 1. From the protected page, click the Profile Icon<br>2. Click the "Log Out" button<br>3. Wait for redirect to the login page<br>4. Press the browser Back button | Navigation back to the protected page is blocked: Auth_Guard redirects to the login page and the protected page is not displayed. The back navigation is effectively blocked and the login page is shown. | medium |
| TC-010 (state_edge) | WF-002 | Log Out in one tab, then attempt Log Out in another tab (concurrent session edge) | User is logged in in two separate browser tabs (Tab A and Tab B) with the same authenticated session | 1. In Tab A, click the Profile Icon<br>2. In Tab A, click the "Log Out" button<br>3. In Tab B, click the Profile Icon<br>4. In Tab B, click the "Log Out" button | Logout in Tab A succeeds: Tab A is redirected to the login page and authentication token cleared. In Tab B, clicking "Log Out" succeeds in resulting in the login page (no error shown) but performs no additional session termination; Tab B is redirected to the login page as well. | medium |
| TC-011 (interaction_edge) | WF-001 | Profile menu and Profile Settings access when user is unauthenticated | User is logged out | 1. Ensure the user is logged out (if not, perform Log Out)<br>2. Observe whether the Profile Icon is visible in the top-right corner<br>3. In the browser address bar, manually navigate to the Profile Settings page URL and press Enter | Profile Icon is not visible when unauthenticated (no dropdown available). Direct navigation to the Profile Settings URL is blocked: Auth_Guard redirects to the login page and the Profile Settings page is not displayed. | medium |
